        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1904138357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1163339961835361913">RELEASED TODAY!!!!! ❤️❤️❤️<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote> “So the rumors about you are true,” he said solemnly.<br/>She swallowed past the lump that had suddenly formed in her throat. “Most of them, I’m afraid.”<br/>“Good.” He continued to hold her gaze when she wished she could look away. “Then be a demon, my beautiful daughter. Be whatever you need to be to put an end to the Kindred once and for all.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509718ra/24983264.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It goes without saying that I’m a rabid fangirl when it comes to the Falling Kingdoms series. It started out with a ‘meh, I don’t </span>
  <span id="freeText1163339961835361913" style="display:none">RELEASED TODAY!!!!! ❤️❤️❤️<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “So the rumors about you are true,” he said solemnly.<br>She swallowed past the lump that had suddenly formed in her throat. “Most of them, I’m afraid.”<br>“Good.” He continued to hold her gaze when she wished she could look away. “Then be a demon, my beautiful daughter. Be whatever you need to be to put an end to the Kindred once and for all.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509718ra/24983264.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It goes without saying that I’m a rabid fangirl when it comes to the Falling Kingdoms series. It started out with a ‘meh, I don’t know if I should continue after this first book’, and now it has [not so] slowly eased its way onto <b>my favorite series of all time list</b>. I’m not kidding when I say that I haven’t added a book to that sucker since 2014 or so. Maybe longer! So, you KNOW it’s a big deal when I choose to add onto it. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “Why did you choose Nic?” Magnus asked, hoping to distract Kyan somehow. “Wasn’t there anyone better?”<br>Kyan laughed. “Nicolo has a soul of fire.”<br>“Because of his hair? More the color of carrots thrown into a horse’s trough than fire, if you ask me.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I’ll admit that it wasn’t a love at first sight type deal, either-besides Magnus (Yeah. More on that morsel later), I just didn’t wholly identify with anyone and <b>not enough happened to satiate my thirst for peril and all things action and violence</b>. If you didn’t know, I can be <i>quite</i> the violent sort when it comes to my books. Ahem…moving on. But, that’s all beside the point, because what have I continually said since I started heavily reviewing on GR? <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Gaius’s eyebrows drew together. He looked pained. “Magnus loved you. He fought for you. He defied me again and again in order to save you, even if it meant his own destruction. He was worthy of you in a way that I was never worthy of Elena. I see that now. And for that alone, you must survive this, Cleiona Bellos.” Then he scowled at her. “But know this. I would personally kill you in an instant if it meant that my son could live again.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>All. I. Need. Is. <i>SOMETHING</i>. To keep me hooked in a book or series</b>. Whether it be something as simple as a tortured look from the male lead, a beautifully written story that keeps my interest if only because it has descriptions that continually draw me in, or so much heart-breaking action that I couldn’t dare to put it down for a moment. It needn’t be huge, but it <i>must</i> be <i>something</i>. In this case? <b>It was all about that dark, hate-to-love, practically forbidden, enemies to lovers romance, baby</b>. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>…<br>Of a beautiful golden princess who rightfully despised him. Whose blue-green eyes held only hate for so long that he didn’t remember precisely when her gaze had softened. <br>This princess who didn’t push him away when he kissed her. Instead, she kissed him back with a passion that very nearly matched his own.<br><i>Perhaps I’m only fantasizing all of it</i>, he thought. </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509388ra/24983234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Sign. Me. UP. <b>I loved my darling Magnus from page one of book one</b>, mmkayyyy? But, unfortunately, there were dual POVs (not a huge fan of this) and I can’t commit to a story that is dull without something to give me hope. And, also unfortunately, it didn’t look like there was going to be any HOPE for my boy…There was just a wee lil smidge of incestual thoughts goin’ on there-and I didn’t see how this was something I could endorse, no matter how much I adored my main man. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He’d also heard of burying a victim in the ground up to their neck, then covering them with tree syrup and allowing a nest of hungry beetles to consume them slowly.<br>That would be nice.<br>Or perhaps Magnus would remove Kurtis’s remaining hand. Saw it off slowly with a dull knife. Or a spoon.<br>Yes, a spoon. </blockquote>
</b><br><br>But then…THEN. This beautiful unicorn of a girl (You know who you are, Bones (LOLZ)) said-<i>’Oh no. No no no. You mustn’t give up. There is a glorious ship. And BOY does it sail. And its not at all like it is now.’</i> So, I persevered-I picked up book two. And, while it certainly wasn’t perfect…far from it…<b>my eyes lit up and my grin went from ear to ear</b>-because there shone a glimmer of hope, right before my moonstruck, rabid fangirly eyes. It wasn’t going to be half bad if this ship sailed.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He needed food. Drink.<br><i>Vengeance</i>.<br>But first and most importantly, he needed to know that Cleo was safe. </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517510651ra/24983351.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then something else happened…and another…then another! The action became breathtaking because I actually cared for more than just one person. The romances began to fly (and die. Then fly again….rinse and repeat). The stories became very interesting. <b>Everything began weaving together so intricately on each page that I couldn’t stop to take a breath</b>. I had a whole new series to devour with endless possibilities…and I had almost put it down forever. <u>Thank God for the power of friendship</u> (and trust bones from Brittney). <br><br>And now, here I am, receiving (and having received) the last two books (FINISHED HARDBACKS!) from the lovely publishers for reviewing, and each time it has made my year. This was just the most wonderful start to 2018 (along with my other favorites so far: Everless, The Cruel Prince, Love, Life and the List…). When I received this book I jumped around, I screamed, I cried…I [attempted] to devour it immediately. I literally bought a book light, people. A BOOK LIGHT-so I could get this sucker done. And I truly wasn’t disappointed. Not by a long shot.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Paelsians burned their dead.<br>Auranians worshipped the goddess of fire and air, so one would think they would fsuavor the Paelsian burial ritual. But rich Auranians favored coffins chiseled from marble, while those of lower status chose wooden boxes.<br>“Kurtis had me buried like an Auranian peasant,” Magnus muttered.<br>Surely, this had to be the former kingsliege’s final insult.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>More than once I couldn’t breathe. More than once I had to put the book down, take a breath, release it, and just try to <i>breathe</i> because <b>my heart was furiously pounding out of my chest, my stomach was in knots</b>…and I just couldn’t even stand it. I <i>might</i> be a bit of a loser when it comes to this series, but I have no regrets-NONE. Frankly, it’s all because of one couple. Let’s be real. And let’s just get down to it:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “I think I scared him.”<br>She nodded. “You can be very scary.”<br>“Yes. And I can also be scared. And I am, right now.” Magnus took her hands in his, his gaze locking with hers. “I want to help you.”<br>Tears welled in her eyes. “I know.”<br>“What do we do, Cleo?” He hated the weakness that had crept into his voice. “How am I supposed to save you from this?” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509388ra/24983235.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Magnus. Magnus and Cleo. I can’t. I truly can’t even. And <b>I suppose I shouldn’t be able to say anything after that ambiguous end to the previous book</b> (OMG I LOVED IT OMG SO EPIC-but perhaps I’m alone in this because, as I’ve stated many a time, I am a masochistic book nerd), but….Morgan Rhodes has released quotes about what we know can’t be the end….so I guess I’m clear??<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “Ashur,” Magnus said with an impatient sigh. I’m going to the palace now. Are you going to join me, or do you wish to call out names while sacrificing random forest creatures?”<br>“You don’t believe,” Ashur said.<br>“What I believe is irrelevant. What I <i>need</i> is to get to Cleo.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>But I’ll be good. So…yeah…ummm….THE REUNION. IS. EVERYTHING. HA! I LIED. Hypothetically, it might have been in a certain jelly situation. <i>Hypothetically</i> it may have taken FOREVER for the two to be in the same damn space and connect and….<i>hypothetically</i>…<b>it might have made my heart stop for a moment</b> (No. For real. Ask my friend, Jen-I literally text her and was like yeah…I need to put this down because the feels have taken over my ability to BREATHE). Ha. But I may be alone here-I think that’s just the possessed fangirl talking again. WHAT. It’s been a YEAR. I’ve waited a YEAR. I can be as happy as I please, thank you very much.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> He knew she was angry with him for scaring Bruno, for acting disrespectful and ungrateful toward Ashur. For wanting to crush anything that stood in the way of finding the answers he needed to save the girl standing before him. <br>To hell with the rest of the world; Cleo was all he cared about. </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509388ra/24983237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>HE didn’t let me down. HE was a perfect husband. HE would do anything for the girl he loves. HE….he would come back from the grave for her-and he shows it tirelessly here. <b>His love is endless and boundless and I adore him</b>. Their love is insurmountable and they’d burn the world down for each other-I truly love this couple and I am going to miss them so so dearly. But isn’t that the best? When a series is large and <u>you STILL didn’t want it to end</u>? That’s only happened here, for me. So, for that, Morgan Rhodes will always be a Rockstar in my eyes. AND-honorable mention: I didn’t care about any of the other POVs before book 5, but in book 5 and this one, they all won me over and I didn’t feel the need for that incessant skimming I did throughout the others-that’s just…it’s amazing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509388ra/24983236.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Now-even though this book is absolute perfection to me, I must mention some things that I [I guesss] weren’t perfect. Okay. I guess there were some things that happened that came off as repetitive. IE they happened a couple too many times? And, even though I loved said thing happening a few times, others might roll their eyes. And I DO think the, ahem, ‘escaping?’ <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[was a bit of an easy cop out <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. That’s not really a spoiler, but I don’t want to hinder anyone’s thoughts on the matter before they go in (I HATE WHEN THAT HAPPENS TO ME AND I ALWAYS COMPLAIN AFTER). I loved that it happened, and I know it couldn’t have happened any other way, but I do wish it would have <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[been more dramatic <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Though…I suppose if I read them back to back, it wouldn’t have mattered because hey, boy went through some Hell, am I right? Perhaps here I was too harsh. And finally, I think I wanted an even BIGGER bang of an end-but, honestly, I still adored it. <br><br>I think I’m still being a pissy pink elephant, though, because I wanted one tiny (it wasn’t tiny) thing to happen that didn’t. BUT it would have ruined the possible HEA so I need to shh. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517509846ra/24983285.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OKAY. Now I’m just rambling. So I’ll end it here. Mags, Cleo, Jonas (my favs the whole time)…Amara, Lucia, Felix, etc. I really did like the end of it all. I really hate long series because, as they progress, they truly do lose something-But that never happened here. In fact, <b>I only loved each installment more and more</b>-so that is something truly special in my eyes. And yes, this is more of a fangirl review and not all poetic and pretty with the words like I know I can do…but sometimes you gotta let that freak flag fly-and if you can’t do it for one of your favorite characters and favorite series of all time…when CAN you do it? If you have read every book and are just waiting on this installment….have fun. I know you will love it, or at least really like it. Not everyone can love all the POVs. If you haven’t read this series? <b>
  <u>Shame on you</u>
</b>. Shame shame shame. If you are considering it? I’ll forgive you. Just this once….but you MUST read it-or I’ll rescind my forgiveness and take all my kindness away lol. Go forth…and enjoy. &lt;3<br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>***************<br><br>Oh guys. This book. You know when it's the final book and nothing can compare to your wild expectations? Well...this is me at work:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516894289ra/24925234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But inside....Inside THIS is me and WAS me the whole entirety of this beautiful novel:<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1516899395ra/24926475.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Because frankly, Magnus has become close to a number one bbf in the span of less than a year. Because this book made it so I literally felt like I couldn't breathe, like the butterflies MIGHT just take over my stomach and come out through my mouth. Because this book, aside from maybe ONE teensy thing I wanted to happen (because, again, I am a masochistic butthole), was everything I could possibly have hoped for. Because this book...<b>it was perfection.</b> <br><br>But like with all wonderful series...I'm sad to see it end. But I couldn't be prouder of this author and how she managed to end with integrity and with a series that never lost steam, but actually GAINED more fans as it progressed. That is SO rare and I am OBSESSED with it. In fact, this might be a top 3 or 4 on my list-and nothing has broken onto that list since, like 2013. So. Yeah.<br><br><br>RTC.<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1871232883" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1871232883" />
    <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines"><img alt="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466111136p2/30004027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1871232883?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines">Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1871232883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6054310696846378744"><blockquote>
  <i>“We cannot be stopped. We are eternal. We are life itself. And we will do anything to survive.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><u>2,5 stars</u><br/><br/>I know it’s time. It’s finally time for me to review this book, which mean <b>it’s also time to say mean things about the last instalment in one of my top 3 favourite series ever</b>. I initially finished this book 3 weeks ago and decided to rate it with a 3.5 stars. But the more I actually tried to write a proper review, the more I realized that I have <u>very few nice things to say about Immortal </u></span>
  <span id="freeText6054310696846378744" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“We cannot be stopped. We are eternal. We are life itself. And we will do anything to survive.”</i>
</blockquote><br><u>2,5 stars</u><br><br>I know it’s time. It’s finally time for me to review this book, which mean <b>it’s also time to say mean things about the last instalment in one of my top 3 favourite series ever</b>. I initially finished this book 3 weeks ago and decided to rate it with a 3.5 stars. But the more I actually tried to write a proper review, the more I realized that I have <u>very few nice things to say about Immortal Reign</u>, therefore I HAD to take-off a full star. Indeed, this book was my most anticipated release of this Fall/Winter season, and it ended up being one of my worst disappointments ever. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520280067ra/25166941.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>First of all I realise that my disappointment is probably due to the <b>lack of memories of the previous instalments</b> (I knew I should have re-read them, I didn’t have the time and now I wish I had). I honestly couldn’t remember the plot, the dynamics or the relationships between the characters. I’m sure my bad brain is one of the main reasons I was not enough invested in this book, BUT there were also some major no-no for me. <b>The book lacked so much depth and was so repetitive</b>; it felt like a running gag, going around in circle, always same-same-same. Same plot, same drama, same deus ex-machina over and over again.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Actually, that was one of my fantasies while in that hateful coffin: marrying you under the blue sky of Auranos in a field of beautiful flowers.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Drama can work (I couldn’t have handled a book without any obstacles) but here, they were not real obstacles, mostly bumps on the roads, <b>easily overcome, even more so forgotten.</b> Action scenes were so fast they became blurred and some events were handled rather unceremoniously. I know before this book started I wished nothing more than Magneo to be okay and Magnus to be happy, and now I can only remember the saying “<i>careful what you wish for</i>”. This book gives us the desired happy ending (and that’s one of the only things I liked in this book) but really, <b>it could have been a bit harder to get there</b> –or the story could have stopped with the previous book altogether– <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520280067ra/25166942.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><u>From this point on, there will be spoilers and disappointments, be warned!</u><br><br>Honestly, so many things piss me off. Starting with Magnus’ ring that seemed to solve every single problem, but also with <b>how forced so many relationship felt</b>. Remind me again why everyone mourned King Gaius? Last book I’ve read, he was a cruel dictator and an abusive father. Why is Lucia part of the heroes? She is as abusive as her father was, and she outdid herself in this book. She did awful things in the name selflessness and yet <b>she was a terrible mother, sister and friend.</b> She got me so mad, always running toward danger without thinking once second about her actions and their consequences. And the abducting felt like a big fat joke, have you try asking if people had your baby before burning the world to the ground? And don’t get me started on Amara and Jonas, they were so useless and boring it made my eyes tear. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“Magnus loved you. He fought for you. He defied me again and again in order to save you, even if it meant his own destruction. He was worthy of you in a way that I was never worthy of Elena. I see that now. And for that alone, you must survive this, Cleiona Bellos.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Overall, <b>this book just lacked</b>. The story lacked spine, the characters lacked humanization and I lacked emotions while reading it. I think I’ll try to go on with my life and tell myself that this book didn’t exist at all. <b>Just pretend that the story ended with Crystal Storm adding there the happy ending</b>, and hope that my mind will be fooled and still love this series. Honestly it won’t be that difficult considering that I already don’t remember much about the book anyways and that even Magus and Cleo were mostly acting out of character.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520280067ra/25166943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>_________________<br><br>Edit January 27, 2017: <b>Magnus, my baby.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460132752ra/18704070.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6054310696846378744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1562473457" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1562473457" />
    <a title="Brittany (Hiatus-On/Off)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off"><img alt="Brittany (Hiatus-On/Off)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469567917p2/5743835.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1562473457?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittany (Hiatus-On/Off)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittany (Hiatus-On/Off)" href="/user/show/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off">Brittany (Hiatus-On/Off)</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off?shelf=all-time-favourites">all-time-favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off?shelf=favourite-authors">favourite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off?shelf=books-with-multi-povs">books-with-multi-povs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5743835-brittany-hiatus-on-off?shelf=books-that-havent-been-released-yet">books-that-havent-been-released-yet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1562473457" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14025958768585655889"><b>Updated March 31st, 2017.</b><br/><br/>The. Cover. Is. <i>PERFECT!</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1490974768l/23367265.jpg' width='400' height='550' alt='image' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I mean it's Magneo! How much better could it get? Please tell me, I want to know!!! <br/><br/>Look at the full wrap around!!! XD XD XD<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491155718i/22381114._SX540_.jpg' width='550' height='300' alt='image' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>January 21st, 2017</b><br/><br/><b>*Note: I typed out this review the day the title for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_' title='Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Falling Kingdoms</a> #6 came out (January 20th, 2017), but I didn’t get to finish it because I had to head to bed and it took me longer than expected to write the review.</b><br/>Okay, there is probably a lot of reviews out for this book tonight...or today? (Here at </span>
  <span id="freeText14025958768585655889" style="display:none"><b>Updated March 31st, 2017.</b><br><br>The. Cover. Is. <i>PERFECT!</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1490974768l/23367265.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="image" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I mean it's Magneo! How much better could it get? Please tell me, I want to know!!! <br><br>Look at the full wrap around!!! XD XD XD<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491155718i/22381114._SX540_.jpg" width="550" height="300" alt="image" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>January 21st, 2017</b><br><br><b>*Note: I typed out this review the day the title for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> #6 came out (January 20th, 2017), but I didn’t get to finish it because I had to head to bed and it took me longer than expected to write the review.</b><br>Okay, there is probably a lot of reviews out for this book tonight...or today? (Here at least it’s nighttime) because the title came out almost five hours ago (would have had my excited title review up sooner but had image troubles...more on that later, and got busy with life), but can I just say how <b>AMAZINGLY AWESOME</b> this title is:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1484961255p8/1804849.jpg" width="480" height="480" alt="image" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It not only sounds and looks (The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> series title's always look so cool and medieval I think) <b>AMAZINGLY AWESOME</b> <i>but</i> it suits the series to perfection I think, too! How cool is that?! Ahhh...I'm getting ahead of myself...let me explain book lovers....<br><br>The first part of the title, <i>IMMORTAL</i> is a perfect word in a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> title because if you have read the series you will most likely know many things in the world of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> are immortal. <br><br>If you haven't read the series I don't want to spoil you by telling you what is immortal...but could I suggest you look into reading the series that is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a>? You won't regret it if you like one of these things or all of them, I promise. Right <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/booksruletheworld" rel="nofollow noopener">Lena</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/may-flower" rel="nofollow noopener">Mayflower</a>? (They were the first two I introduced to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a>). If you like multiple POV's, magic, suspense beyond the edge of your seat, characters that make you want to jump inside the book and help them, wrap them up in a blanket, (My little M baby! ^^) I didn't want to say the character's name because I want to see if you will fall for the unknown character too, I didn’t at first, but now...I wish I was best friends with M and especially Cleo! I could kick butt with Cleo, help and be strong with M), say ASJKD to them and the situations they are in or <i>get</i> in (Jonas, love you buddy), strangle them, laugh out loud with them and have one, no, actual several <b>AMAZINGLY AWESOME</b> adventures with them then you will like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a>! <br><br>If you cannot tell, this series has made me into the fangirl I am today and helped me begin to understand the fangirl language. This book and all of my book loving friends have helped me, actually. I am grateful to every single one of you for being my friend. *Hugs* Seriously before them and this series I was lost in the world of fangirling. I was <i>real</i> lost. If you don't believe me, ask <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/booksruletheworld" rel="nofollow noopener">Lena</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/may-flower" rel="nofollow noopener">Mayflower</a>, the friends of many I introduced to this series. (Just to let you know, I can’t stop recommending this series if you cannot tell. Also to let you know, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/may-flower" rel="nofollow noopener">Mayflower</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/booksruletheworld" rel="nofollow noopener">Lena</a> are <i>happy</i> or is it very <i>emotional</i> I put them through that 5th book cliffhanger? I don’t know. Maybe when I read the 5th book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367261.Crystal_Storm__Falling_Kingdoms___5_" title="Crystal Storm (Falling Kingdoms, #5) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Crystal Storm</a> I will understand.)<br><br>Okay I got a bit side tracked, back to the title now. The second part of the title, <i>REIGN</i> is a perfect word in a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> title because reign is to do with kingdoms, princes, kings, princesses, queens and ruling or reigning and what does the world of FK have? All of that and MORE. <br><br>SO. <br><br>MUCH. <br><br><i>MORE!</i><br><br>So back to the beginning of my review, how cool is that title?!? <b>AMAZINGLY AWESOME COOL</b> is what I think that title is! I couldn’t ask for a better title to finish the world of FK (It’s the last book, I can’t believe it!) What about you, what do you think of the title? Do you think it suits the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> series from what I told you above?<br><br>Thank you for reading my first fangirl book title review on the book title, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367265.Immortal_Reign__Falling_Kingdoms___6_" title="Immortal Reign (Falling Kingdoms, #6) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortal Reign</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> book number six. Hope you enjoyed it. I certainly enjoyed writing it. (Tonight I was freaking out about this title if you cannot tell from above…)<br><br>Oh. I almost forgot! My image troubles were saved by my new book loving friend, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/AsThePlotThickens" rel="nofollow noopener">Coreen &lt;3 (As the Plot Thickens)</a>. Who, very kindly gave me the correct link to the FK #6 title image and the numbers to size it so I could put it into my review to admire and for other book lovers to admire too. Thank you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/AsThePlotThickens" rel="nofollow noopener">Coreen &lt;3 (As the Plot Thickens)</a>. <br><br>Wait. Am I not forgetting something important? The release date <i>December 2017</i> almost a year away, how am I going to live that long? Well, I’m going to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22571365.A_Book_of_Spirits_and_Thieves__Spirits_and_Thieves___1_" title="A Book of Spirits and Thieves (Spirits and Thieves, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">A Book of Spirits and Thieves</a> and its sequel <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367270.The_Darkest_Magic__Spirits_and_Thieves___2_" title="The Darkest Magic (Spirits and Thieves, #2) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Magic</a> and the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12954620.Falling_Kingdoms__Falling_Kingdoms___1_" title="Falling Kingdoms (Falling Kingdoms, #1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> novellas, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32597619.Obsidian_Blade" title="Obsidian Blade by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian Blade</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31434056.Crimson_Dagger_Part_I__Falling_Kingdoms___0_1_" title="Crimson Dagger Part I (Falling Kingdoms, #0.1) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Crimson Dagger</a>, discover new books <i>and</i> I’m going to fangirl over how much I love this series and its new title, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367265.Immortal_Reign__Falling_Kingdoms___6_" title="Immortal Reign (Falling Kingdoms, #6) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortal Reign</a>! Who’s with me? All book lovers are welcome and also happy for newcomers.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18364870592427783454">A MILLION AND ONE STARS<br/><br/>This gem of a series just tore me up inside out and I sincerely thank Morgan Rhodes for that and for rendering me completely useless for conversation until I finished reading.<br/><br/>I just love this series so hard and I couldn’t wish for a better ending. I couldn’t tell you how many times I’ve read the last chapter. Trying my best to soak in every little details that made my heart so full.<br/><br/>Alright I’m having feels again and that’s my cue.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8447842352973643853"><blockquote> <i> <b>I've found that in my life that love and attraction can take many forms. And if one is open to unexpected possibilities, there are no boundaries.</b></i> (copied from Goodreads 😆)</blockquote>I failed to see why Morgan Rhodes delayed this book to "make it more memorable" for us readers. It was good. But not in the way it should have been. I am not satisfied. I read this two months ago. I don’t remember few things I wanted to talk about. And I didn't take any notes. Anyway, I'm still gonna review it. <br/>=> First quart</span>
  <span id="freeText8447842352973643853" style="display:none"><blockquote> <i> <b>I've found that in my life that love and attraction can take many forms. And if one is open to unexpected possibilities, there are no boundaries.</b></i> (copied from Goodreads 😆)</blockquote>I failed to see why Morgan Rhodes delayed this book to "make it more memorable" for us readers. It was good. But not in the way it should have been. I am not satisfied. I read this two months ago. I don’t remember few things I wanted to talk about. And I didn't take any notes. Anyway, I'm still gonna review it. <br />=&gt; First quarter of the book is literally amazing. I enjoyed it alot.<br />=&gt; The only thing which was unpredictable for me was the mystery of Lissa's kidnapping. <br />=&gt; I failed to see why Morgan Rhodes didn't unite Jonas and Lucia <i>clearly</i>. It seemed like they wanted to be close but author didn't wanted them to be. <br />=&gt; In the entire <i>effing</i> series, Amara seemed to be an enemy. Sub-antagonist. But this novel, made her a kind of sub-heroine. I am neither disliking this fact nor liking. I am confused what the heck she was?!<br />=&gt; I got very confused about Nerissa in this novel. I didn't expect that. It was very sudden, in my opinion. Anyway, okay..😞<br />=&gt; Magnus and Cleo. I loved their every scene. But sometimes Magnus became over protective. Understood but annoyed me a bit.<br /><br />That's all I can remember for now. It was a good series but I didn't like this part that much. <br />I beg to Morgan Rhodes, please release the conclusion novel of Spirit and Thieves series this year. I haven't read the Darkest Magic yet. But will very soon. <br /> <br />22 May, 2018</span>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=otps-feels">otps-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1796111149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9958150286342919910">A proper end to a high-stakes, action-packed journey filled with secrets, betrayal, hate, love, friendship, forgiveness, and redemption.<br/><br/><b>Relationships:</b><br/><u> Magnus & Cleo </u> <br/>As I've said in previous reviews, I would literally sacrifice all the other characters if it meant these two were alive and happy. And while I certainly found myself liking the other characters more this time around, I stand by that statement lol. Fortunately, it did not come to that. <br/><br/>In the words of King Gaius: <br/><i> “Magnus loved you. </i></span>
  <span id="freeText9958150286342919910" style="display:none">A proper end to a high-stakes, action-packed journey filled with secrets, betrayal, hate, love, friendship, forgiveness, and redemption.<br /><br /><b>Relationships:</b><br /><u> Magnus &amp; Cleo </u> <br />As I've said in previous reviews, I would literally sacrifice all the other characters if it meant these two were alive and happy. And while I certainly found myself liking the other characters more this time around, I stand by that statement lol. Fortunately, it did not come to that. <br /><br />In the words of King Gaius: <br /><i> “Magnus loved you. He fought for you. He defied me again and again in order to save you, even if it meant his own destruction. He was worthy of you in a way that I was never worthy of Elena. I see that now. And for that alone, you must survive this, Cleiona Bellos.” </i> <br /><br /><u>Jonas &amp; Lucia</u> <br />No joke, Jonas might be the most forgiving guy in the history of ever. Despite everything Lucia does he stands by her, constantly believes in her and he saves her countless times. Even after she does something stupid and betrays his trust he is quick to forgive her. While they don't have any particularly romance-centric scenes, I think it is safe to say they become more than friends by the end. In some ways, I think Jonas becomes to Lucia, what Cleo is to Magnus, her light. Someone who knows the horrible things she's done, the darkness she has in her, and isn't afraid, who continues to see the goodness in her and fight for her. <br /><br /><br />*More Detailed review to Come*</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1808436530" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer211143097213803083"><i>”She was his goddess. His love. His life. And he would do anything to save her.”</i><br/><br/>1) Falling kingdoms ★★★<br/>2) Rebel spring ★★★<br/>3) Gathering darkness ★★★★<br/>4) Frozen tides ★★★★★<br/>5) Crystal storm ★★★★★<br/><br/><b>4.5</b><br/><br/>Well, where to begin? Just kidding, I'm obviously going to begin with what makes this series great: <b>M A G N E O.</b> Magnus and Cleo. The <s>prince</s> king of sass and the <s>princess </s> ray of sunshine.<br/>They're what convinced me to keep reading these books, <b>they're the heart of the story</b> and I'm so happy they got the ha</span>
  <span id="freeText211143097213803083" style="display:none"><i>”She was his goddess. His love. His life. And he would do anything to save her.”</i><br /><br />1) Falling kingdoms ★★★<br />2) Rebel spring ★★★<br />3) Gathering darkness ★★★★<br />4) Frozen tides ★★★★★<br />5) Crystal storm ★★★★★<br /><br /><b>4.5</b><br /><br />Well, where to begin? Just kidding, I'm obviously going to begin with what makes this series great: <b>M A G N E O.</b> Magnus and Cleo. The <s>prince</s> king of sass and the <s>princess </s> ray of sunshine.<br />They're what convinced me to keep reading these books, <b>they're the heart of the story</b> and I'm so happy they got the happy ending they deserved.<br />Their reunion? Perfect<br />Their last scene? Perfect<br />Every single one of their interactions? Perfect<br />Honestly, the entire series could just be about them thinking about how much they despise each other but secretly making out passive aggressively and I'd be in heaven.<br /><br /><b>Plus, the impossible happened: I stopped hating Jonas and Lucia.</b><br />Yes, I know, incredible.<br />They finally stopped being angsty and stupid teenagers, they grew up and started using their brains (<i>!!!!!</i>), I almost feel proud.<br /><br />The only reason I didn't give Immortal reign five full stars is that <b>the ending was a bit too convenient and fast,</b> I wish Morgan Rhodes would have added a few more chapters to show us what all the characters are up to.<br /><br />But <b>it was a very satisfying conclusion,</b> I don't want to say goodbye to these amazing world and characters (<i>yeah I'm just talking about Magnus and Cleo</i>), I hope Morgan Rhodes will give us some novellas or spin offs!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oW8X4Sn8KAOHsjUC2MoW53YHRI7J3lAQBAnS9Py95bD72vEWv/erv9jRN3wU+CWxC1UDzVLm4yVf4OxhXzRh/A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b8PN3KeD7b190Kkx4Kn/GNTD2eMQXmGq1Wre3N9xaPU1disrMYhuASKzq08sm8xOqZGeoItm0p+Og+BJfPjsuQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7640814552995825238">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText7640814552995825238" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>
